        assert cmd[sandbox_idx + 1] == "workspace-write"
        assert "-c" in cmd
        config_idx = cmd.index("-c")
        assert cmd[config_idx + 1] == 'model_reasoning_effort="high"'
        assert "--output-last-message" in cmd
        idx = cmd.index("--output-last-message")
        assert cmd[idx + 1] == str(out)
        assert cmd[-1] == "hello"

    def test_format_agent_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import format_agent_header

        assert (
            format_agent_header("claude", "opus")
            == "[Mopsus Oracle | Claude opus]"
        )
        assert (
            format_agent_header("codex", "gpt-5-codex")
            == "[Patchsmith | Codex gpt-5-codex]"
        )


class TestSoulPrompt:
    def test_soul_prompt_included_in_command(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
            "soul_prompt": "I am Mopsus, a wise oracle.",
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        idx = cmd.index("--append-system-prompt")
        assert cmd[idx + 1] == "I am Mopsus, a wise oracle."

    def test_soul_prompt_absent_when_empty(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
            "soul_prompt": "",
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        assert "--append-system-prompt" not in cmd

    def test_soul_prompt_absent_when_missing(self):
        from mopsus.agent import build_claude_command

        config = {
            "permission_mode": "default",
            "allowed_tools": "Read,Glob",
            "allow_dangerous": False,
        }
        cmd = build_claude_command("opus", None, config)
        assert "--append-system-prompt" not in cmd

    def test_get_config_loads_soul_file(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        soul_file = tmp_path / "soul.md"
        soul_file.write_text("I am the oracle.\n")
        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == "I am the oracle."

    def test_get_config_missing_soul_file(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == ""


class TestConfigAndModelSelection:
    def test_get_config_invalid_default_model_falls_back(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_DEFAULT_MODEL": "invalid-model",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["default_model"] == "opus"

    def test_get_config_sets_default_codex_model(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_model"] == "gpt-5-codex"
            assert config["codex_sandbox"] == "workspace-write"
            assert config["codex_reasoning_effort"] == "high"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_bin(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_BIN": "/Users/v/.bun/bin/codex",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_bin"] == "/Users/v/.bun/bin/codex"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_sandbox(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_SANDBOX": "read-only",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_sandbox"] == "read-only"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_reasoning_effort(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_REASONING_EFFORT": "medium",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_reasoning_effort"] == "medium"

    def test_get_config_loads_distinct_claude_and_codex_prompts(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        (tmp_path / "soul.md").write_text("Claude soul")
        (tmp_path / "situation.md").write_text("Claude situation")
        (tmp_path / "codex_soul.md").write_text("Codex soul")
        (tmp_path / "codex_situation.md").write_text("Codex situation")

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == "Claude soul\n\nClaude situation"
            assert config["codex_prompt"] == "Codex soul\n\nCodex situation"
            assert config["claude_prompt_files"] == ["soul.md", "situation.md"]
            assert config["codex_prompt_files"] == [
                "codex_soul.md",
                "codex_situation.md",
            ]

    def test_run_claude_uses_config_default_for_new_chat(self):
        from mopsus.agent import run_claude

        config = {"default_model": "sonnet", "allow_dangerous": False}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.get_session",
                    return_value={"session_id": None, "model": "opus"},
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.has_chat_state", return_value=False),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_claude_once",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "sess-new")),
                ) as mocked_run_once,
                patch("mopsus.agent.set_session_id") as mocked_set_session,
            ):
                response, session_id = await run_claude("hello", 123, config)
                mocked_run_once.assert_awaited_once_with(
                    "hello", "sonnet", None, config
                )
                mocked_set_session.assert_called_once_with(123, "sess-new")
                assert response == "ok"
                assert session_id == "sess-new"

        asyncio.run(_exercise())

    def test_voice_message_stub_is_reachable(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = None
                self.voice = object()
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(bot_data={"config": {}}, bot=SimpleNamespace())

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await handle_message(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert update.message.replies == ["Voice messages are not supported yet."]


class TestHelpCommand:
    def test_help_command_returns_usage(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_help

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={"config": {"broadcast_mode": True, "chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}}
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await cmd_help(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert update.message.replies
        body = update.message.replies[0]
        assert "/help" in body
        assert "/status" in body
        assert "/codex <prompt>" in body
        assert "Broadcast mode: ON" in body

    def test_help_command_uses_effective_message(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_help

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        effective_message = DummyMessage()
        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            effective_message=effective_message,
            message=None,
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={"config": {"broadcast_mode": True, "chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}}
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await cmd_help(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert effective_message.replies
        assert "Mopsus Help" in effective_message.replies[0]
        assert "Claude+Codex when broadcast is ON" in effective_message.replies[0]


class TestMessageRouting:
    def test_plain_text_broadcasts_to_both_backends(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = "hello team"
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": True,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ) as mocked_backend,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                assert mocked_backend.await_count == 2
                called_backends = [
                    call.kwargs["backend"] for call in mocked_backend.await_args_list
                ]
                assert called_backends == ["claude", "codex"]

        asyncio.run(_exercise())

    def test_explicit_codex_stays_single_backend(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = "codex: quick check"
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": True,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ) as mocked_backend,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                assert mocked_backend.await_count == 1
                assert mocked_backend.await_args_list[0].kwargs["backend"] == "codex"

        asyncio.run(_exercise())


class TestTypingLoop:
    def test_typing_loop_tolerates_timeout(self):
        from telegram.error import TimedOut

        from mopsus.agent import _typing_loop

        class DummyBot:
            def __init__(self):
                self.calls = 0

            async def send_chat_action(self, chat_id: int, action: str):
                self.calls += 1
                if self.calls == 1:
                    raise TimedOut("Timed out")
                raise asyncio.CancelledError

        bot = DummyBot()

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.asyncio.sleep", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)):
                await _typing_loop(bot, 123)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert bot.calls == 2


class TestBackendAnnouncements:
    def test_codex_response_includes_speaker_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import _run_backend_request

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.placeholder = SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                return self.placeholder

        message = DummyMessage()
        bot = SimpleNamespace(send_message=AsyncMock(), send_chat_action=AsyncMock())
        config = {"default_model": "opus", "codex_model": "gpt-5-codex"}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.run_codex", new=AsyncMock(return_value="Implemented.")
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent._typing_loop", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)),
            ):
                await _run_backend_request(
                    backend="codex",
                    prompt="do thing",
                    chat_id=123,
                    message=message,
                    bot=bot,
                    config=config,
                )

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        sent = message.placeholder.edit_text.await_args.args[0]
        assert sent.startswith("<b>[Patchsmith | Codex gpt-5-codex]</b>")

    def test_claude_response_includes_speaker_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import _run_backend_request

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.placeholder = SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                return self.placeholder

        message = DummyMessage()
        bot = SimpleNamespace(send_message=AsyncMock(), send_chat_action=AsyncMock())
        config = {"default_model": "sonnet", "codex_model": "gpt-5-codex"}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.run_claude",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("All set.", None)),
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.has_chat_state", return_value=False),
                patch("mopsus.agent._typing_loop", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)),
            ):
                await _run_backend_request(
                    backend="claude",
                    prompt="do thing",
                    chat_id=123,
                    message=message,
                    bot=bot,
                    config=config,
                )

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        sent = message.placeholder.edit_text.await_args.args[0]
        assert sent.startswith("<b>[Mopsus Oracle | Claude sonnet]</b>")


Turn 1 - Assistant
**Decision Diff (from RFC)**
- `+ #1 _env_choice`: implement now. Low risk, real duplication cut in [`mopsus/agent.py`](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/mopsus/agent.py).
- `~ #2 authenticated decorator`: defer as-is; replace with a plain helper now (`require_auth_and_message`) instead of decorator magic. Same dedup, less indirection risk in async handlers.
- `+ #3 _record_blackboard`: implement now. Good dedup and easier future backend extension.
- `- #4 delete parse_backend_request`: do **not** delete now; tests and possible external callers still use it. Keep as compatibility shim, mark deprecated.
- `+ #5 response formatting cleanup`: implement now.
- `- #6 setdefault for lock`: reject. `setdefault(..., asyncio.Lock())` constructs a lock every call; current explicit form is safer/clearer.
- `~ #7 simplify get_reply_message with or`: partial. Add return type annotation now, keep explicit `is not None` logic for safety.
- `+ #8 return type annotation`: implement now (`-> Message | None`).
- `- #9 remove redundant or ""`: defer. Keeping null-tolerant cleanup is defensive hardening, not harmful complexity.

**Premise Check**
- Cutting ~100 LOC is not the real complexity win.
- Real complexity is control-flow branching across auth, routing, queueing, and blackboard side effects.
- Prioritize simplifications that reduce branching and side-effect duplication, not just line count.

**Reliability Guardrails**
- Add regression tests before refactor:
  - Unauthorized command behavior across all handlers.
  - `parse_backend_request` compatibility.
  - Blackboard writes for `/codex` and broadcast turns.
  - Lock identity/stability per chat.
- Roll out in 2 commits:
  1. Pure helpers + no behavior change.
  2. Handler rewiring to helper/decorator equivalent.
- Keep `parse_backend_request` for one release with deprecation note in docstring.

**Radical Option (risky, high payoff)**
- Replace per-command branching with one `TurnContext` pipeline:
  - `ingest -> auth -> route -> execute -> persist -> render`.
- Move backend-specific behavior behind a `BackendRunner` interface (`claude`, `codex`) so routing has zero backend `if/else`.
- Split [`mopsus/agent.py`](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/mopsus/agent.py) into `config.py`, `routing.py`, `handlers.py`, `backends/`, `blackboard.py`.
- Risk: larger change surface now; payoff: major future reliability and testability gains.

If you want, I can produce a concrete “Phase 1 patch plan” (function-by-function edit list + corresponding test deltas) in diff format next.

### Agent A · `gpt-5.3-codex` · 27s

Your revision is strong. One assumption to challenge: `_chat_locks` is effectively bounded today because auth gates to one configured `chat_id`, so lock-eviction is not urgent unless multi-chat support is planned.

Revised call:

1. Implement now: `#1`, `#2` (plain helper, not decorator), `#3`, `#5`, `#8`, `#9`.
2. `#4`: choose one explicit path now.
   - Preferred: delete `parse_backend_request` and update tests.
   - Conservative: keep shim with `DeprecationWarning` and hard removal date (for example, April 1, 2026).
3. `#6`: keep explicit `_get_lock` for clarity or use `setdefault`; reliability impact is negligible either way.
4. `#7`: keep explicit `is not None` logic; add return type annotation without switching to `or`.

Non-obvious reliability simplification to consider now:

1. Stop broadcast-by-default and require explicit dual-run (`/both` or prefix). This removes the highest side-effect multiplier.
2. Introduce a small `TurnContext` object and one shared `process_turn()` path used by `/codex` and text handling. This shrinks branching more than line-level cleanup.
3. Add one policy test: “one user input -> exactly N blackboard writes where N = selected backends + user row.” That catches most regressions from refactors.

If you want, I can draft a concrete phase plan with exact function signatures and test edits.

# RFC: agent.py simplification

**Date:** 2026-02-26
**File:** `mopsus/agent.py` (1254 lines)
**Author:** Claude Opus 4.6

---

## Summary

Nine refactoring suggestions for `mopsus/agent.py` that together remove ~100 lines of code with zero behavioral change. Ordered by impact.

---

## 1. Extract `_env_choice` helper (~20 lines saved)

The same validate-warn-fallback pattern for env vars repeats 3 times in `get_config()`. A small helper collapses all three.

**Add near `_env_bool` (line 77):**

```python
def _env_choice(name: str, valid: set[str], default: str, *, lower: bool = True) -> str:
    """Read an env var, validate against a set of choices, warn and fall back."""
    raw = os.environ.get(name, default).strip()
    if lower:
        raw = raw.lower()
    if raw in valid:
        return raw
    log.warning("Invalid %s=%r; falling back to %r", name, raw, default)
    return default
```

**Then replace lines 158-185 with:**

```python
default_model = _env_choice("MOPSUS_DEFAULT_MODEL", VALID_MODELS, "opus")
codex_model = os.environ.get("MOPSUS_CODEX_MODEL", DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL).strip() or DEFAULT_CODEX_MODEL
codex_sandbox = _env_choice(
    "MOPSUS_CODEX_SANDBOX",
    {"read-only", "workspace-write", "danger-full-access"},
    "workspace-write",
    lower=False,
)
codex_reasoning_effort = _env_choice(
    "MOPSUS_CODEX_REASONING_EFFORT",
    {"low", "medium", "high"},
    "high",
)
```

---

## 2. Extract `@authenticated` decorator (~35 lines saved)

Five command handlers (`cmd_reset`, `cmd_model`, `cmd_status`, `cmd_help`, `cmd_codex`) repeat the same 7-line auth+message guard preamble.

**Add after `get_reply_message`:**

```python
from functools import wraps

def authenticated(handler):
    """Decorator that checks auth and resolves the reply message."""
    @wraps(handler)
    async def wrapper(update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        config = context.bot_data["config"]
        message = get_reply_message(update)
        if (err := check_auth(update, config)):
            if message is not None:
                await message.reply_text(err)
            return
        if message is None:
            return
        await handler(update, context, config=config, message=message)
    return wrapper
```

**Example rewrite of `cmd_help`:**

```python
@authenticated
async def cmd_help(update, context, *, config, message):
    broadcast = "ON" if config.get("broadcast_mode") else "off"
    lines = [...]
    await message.reply_text("\n".join(lines))
```

Note: `cmd_reset` accesses `message` after the guard but with its own `if message is not None` check -- it would need a slightly different treatment or could just use the decorator and pass `message` through.

Note: `handle_message` has the same preamble but also does `chat_id` extraction and voice checks between the auth guard and the main logic, so it may not benefit from the decorator as cleanly.

---

## 3. Extract `_record_blackboard` helper (~30 lines saved)

Both `cmd_codex` (lines 1079-1105) and `handle_message` (lines 1150-1178) repeat the same blackboard-write pattern for user input and assistant output.

**Add as a module-level helper:**

```python
def _record_blackboard(chat_id: int, role: str, backend: str, text: str,
                       config: dict, model: str | None = None) -> None:
    """Append a blackboard entry if the blackboard is enabled."""
    if not config.get("blackboard_enabled", True):
        return
    append_blackboard_entry(
        chat_id,
        role=role,
        backend=backend,
        model=model,
        text=text,
        max_entries=max(1, int(config.get("blackboard_max_entries", 60))),
    )
```

**Then each call site reduces from 8 lines to 1:**

```python
_record_blackboard(chat_id, "user", "user", prompt, config)
# ... run backend ...
_record_blackboard(chat_id, "assistant", backend, raw_response, config, model=model)
```

---

## 4. Delete dead `parse_backend_request` (10 lines)

`parse_backend_request` at line 598 is a thin wrapper around `parse_backend_request_details` that discards the third return value. It is never called anywhere in the file. Delete lines 598-607.

---

## 5. Simplify `_run_backend_request` response formatting (5 lines)

Lines 1043-1044 have an unnecessary intermediate variable:

```python
raw_response = response_text or ""
response_body = (response_text or "").lstrip("\r\n")
```

Simplify to:

```python
raw_response = response_text or ""
response_body = raw_response.lstrip("\r\n")
```

The `.lstrip("\r\n")` guard for a response that is entirely whitespace is borderline unnecessary but harmless. The key fix is removing the redundant `(response_text or "")` when `raw_response` already holds that value.

---

## 6. Use `setdefault` in `_get_lock` (2 lines)

Lines 845-848:

```python
def _get_lock(chat_id: int) -> asyncio.Lock:
    if chat_id not in _chat_locks:
        _chat_locks[chat_id] = asyncio.Lock()
    return _chat_locks[chat_id]
```

Replace with:

```python
def _get_lock(chat_id: int) -> asyncio.Lock:
    return _chat_locks.setdefault(chat_id, asyncio.Lock())
```

Lock creation is trivially cheap; this is idiomatic Python.

---

## 7. Simplify `get_reply_message` with `or` (3 lines)

Lines 246-251:

```python
def get_reply_message(update: Update):
    """Return the best available message object for replying."""
    message = getattr(update, "effective_message", None)
    if message is not None:
        return message
    return getattr(update, "message", None)
```

Replace with:

```python
def get_reply_message(update: Update) -> Message | None:
    """Return the best available message object for replying."""
    return getattr(update, "effective_message", None) or getattr(update, "message", None)
```

(This also addresses suggestion 8 below.)

---

## 8. Add return type annotation to `get_reply_message`

Every other top-level function in the file has a return type. Add `-> Message | None` (requires `from telegram import Message` in the imports). Covered by the rewrite in suggestion 7.

---

## 9. Remove redundant `or ""` in `_clean_blackboard_text`

Line 343:

```python
cleaned = " ".join((text or "").replace("\r", "\n").split())
```

The parameter is typed `str`, so it can never be `None`. Simplify to:

```python
cleaned = " ".join(text.replace("\r", "\n").split())
```

---

## Impact summary

| # | Suggestion | Lines saved | Benefit |
|---|-----------|-------------|---------|
| 1 | `_env_choice` helper | ~20 | Eliminates 3x validate-warn-fallback |
| 2 | `@authenticated` decorator | ~35 | Removes boilerplate from 5 handlers |
| 3 | `_record_blackboard` helper | ~30 | Deduplicates blackboard writes |
| 4 | Delete dead `parse_backend_request` | 10 | Dead code removal |
| 5 | Simplify response formatting | 5 | Remove redundant expression |
| 6 | `setdefault` for locks | 2 | Idiomatic Python |
| 7 | Simplify `get_reply_message` | 3 | Clearer intent |
| 8 | Add return type annotation | 0 | Type consistency |
| 9 | Remove redundant `or ""` | 0 | Accuracy to type contract |

**Total: ~100 lines removed, zero behavioral change.**
