        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_BIN": "/Users/v/.bun/bin/codex",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_bin"] == "/Users/v/.bun/bin/codex"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_sandbox(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_SANDBOX": "read-only",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_sandbox"] == "read-only"

    def test_get_config_prefers_configured_codex_reasoning_effort(self):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
            "MOPSUS_CODEX_REASONING_EFFORT": "medium",
        }
        with patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["codex_reasoning_effort"] == "medium"

    def test_get_config_loads_distinct_claude_and_codex_prompts(self, tmp_path):
        from mopsus.agent import get_config

        (tmp_path / "soul.md").write_text("Claude soul")
        (tmp_path / "situation.md").write_text("Claude situation")
        (tmp_path / "codex_soul.md").write_text("Codex soul")
        (tmp_path / "codex_situation.md").write_text("Codex situation")

        fake_env = {
            "MOPSUS_BOT_TOKEN": "token",
            "MOPSUS_CHAT_ID": "123",
        }
        with (
            patch.dict(os.environ, fake_env, clear=True),
            patch("mopsus.agent.REPO_DIR", tmp_path),
        ):
            config = get_config()
            assert config["soul_prompt"] == "Claude soul\n\nClaude situation"
            assert config["codex_prompt"] == "Codex soul\n\nCodex situation"
            assert config["claude_prompt_files"] == ["soul.md", "situation.md"]
            assert config["codex_prompt_files"] == [
                "codex_soul.md",
                "codex_situation.md",
            ]

    def test_run_claude_uses_config_default_for_new_chat(self):
        from mopsus.agent import run_claude

        config = {"default_model": "sonnet", "allow_dangerous": False}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.get_session",
                    return_value={"session_id": None, "model": "opus"},
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.has_chat_state", return_value=False),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_claude_once",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "sess-new")),
                ) as mocked_run_once,
                patch("mopsus.agent.set_session_id") as mocked_set_session,
            ):
                response, session_id = await run_claude("hello", 123, config)
                mocked_run_once.assert_awaited_once_with(
                    "hello", "sonnet", None, config
                )
                mocked_set_session.assert_called_once_with(123, "sess-new")
                assert response == "ok"
                assert session_id == "sess-new"

        asyncio.run(_exercise())

    def test_voice_message_stub_is_reachable(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = None
                self.voice = object()
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(bot_data={"config": {}}, bot=SimpleNamespace())

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await handle_message(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert update.message.replies == ["Voice messages are not supported yet."]


class TestHelpCommand:
    def test_help_command_returns_usage(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_help

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={"config": {"broadcast_mode": True, "chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}}
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await cmd_help(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert update.message.replies
        body = update.message.replies[0]
        assert "/help" in body
        assert "/status" in body
        assert "/codex <prompt>" in body
        assert "Broadcast mode: ON" in body

    def test_help_command_uses_effective_message(self):
        from mopsus.agent import cmd_help

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        effective_message = DummyMessage()
        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            effective_message=effective_message,
            message=None,
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={"config": {"broadcast_mode": True, "chat_id": 100, "user_id": None}}
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None):
                await cmd_help(update, context)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert effective_message.replies
        assert "Mopsus Help" in effective_message.replies[0]
        assert "Claude+Codex when broadcast is ON" in effective_message.replies[0]


class TestMessageRouting:
    def test_plain_text_broadcasts_to_both_backends(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = "hello team"
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": True,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ) as mocked_backend,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                assert mocked_backend.await_count == 2
                called_backends = [
                    call.kwargs["backend"] for call in mocked_backend.await_args_list
                ]
                assert called_backends == ["claude", "codex"]

        asyncio.run(_exercise())

    def test_explicit_codex_stays_single_backend(self):
        from mopsus.agent import handle_message

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.text = "codex: quick check"
                self.voice = None
                self.audio = None
                self.replies: list[str] = []

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                self.replies.append(text)
                return SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

        update = SimpleNamespace(
            effective_chat=SimpleNamespace(id=100),
            effective_user=SimpleNamespace(id=200),
            message=DummyMessage(),
        )
        context = SimpleNamespace(
            bot_data={
                "config": {
                    "broadcast_mode": True,
                    "blackboard_enabled": False,
                    "chat_id": 100,
                    "user_id": None,
                }
            },
            bot=SimpleNamespace(),
        )

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch("mopsus.agent.check_auth", return_value=None),
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent._run_backend_request",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("ok", "model")),
                ) as mocked_backend,
            ):
                await handle_message(update, context)
                assert mocked_backend.await_count == 1
                assert mocked_backend.await_args_list[0].kwargs["backend"] == "codex"

        asyncio.run(_exercise())


class TestTypingLoop:
    def test_typing_loop_tolerates_timeout(self):
        from telegram.error import TimedOut

        from mopsus.agent import _typing_loop

        class DummyBot:
            def __init__(self):
                self.calls = 0

            async def send_chat_action(self, chat_id: int, action: str):
                self.calls += 1
                if self.calls == 1:
                    raise TimedOut("Timed out")
                raise asyncio.CancelledError

        bot = DummyBot()

        async def _exercise():
            with patch("mopsus.agent.asyncio.sleep", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)):
                await _typing_loop(bot, 123)

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        assert bot.calls == 2


class TestBackendAnnouncements:
    def test_codex_response_includes_speaker_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import _run_backend_request

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.placeholder = SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                return self.placeholder

        message = DummyMessage()
        bot = SimpleNamespace(send_message=AsyncMock(), send_chat_action=AsyncMock())
        config = {"default_model": "opus", "codex_model": "gpt-5-codex"}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.run_codex", new=AsyncMock(return_value="Implemented.")
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent._typing_loop", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)),
            ):
                await _run_backend_request(
                    backend="codex",
                    prompt="do thing",
                    chat_id=123,
                    message=message,
                    bot=bot,
                    config=config,
                )

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        sent = message.placeholder.edit_text.await_args.args[0]
        assert sent.startswith("<b>[Patchsmith | Codex gpt-5-codex]</b>")

    def test_claude_response_includes_speaker_header(self):
        from mopsus.agent import _run_backend_request

        class DummyMessage:
            def __init__(self):
                self.placeholder = SimpleNamespace(edit_text=AsyncMock())

            async def reply_text(self, text: str):
                return self.placeholder

        message = DummyMessage()
        bot = SimpleNamespace(send_message=AsyncMock(), send_chat_action=AsyncMock())
        config = {"default_model": "sonnet", "codex_model": "gpt-5-codex"}

        async def _exercise():
            with (
                patch(
                    "mopsus.agent.run_claude",
                    new=AsyncMock(return_value=("All set.", None)),
                ),
                patch("mopsus.agent.has_chat_state", return_value=False),
                patch("mopsus.agent._typing_loop", new=AsyncMock(return_value=None)),
            ):
                await _run_backend_request(
                    backend="claude",
                    prompt="do thing",
                    chat_id=123,
                    message=message,
                    bot=bot,
                    config=config,
                )

        asyncio.run(_exercise())
        sent = message.placeholder.edit_text.await_args.args[0]
        assert sent.startswith("<b>[Mopsus Oracle | Claude sonnet]</b>")


Here is the first proposal:

**Decision Diff (from RFC)**
- `+ #1 _env_choice`: implement now. Low risk, real duplication cut in [`mopsus/agent.py`](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/mopsus/agent.py).
- `~ #2 authenticated decorator`: defer as-is; replace with a plain helper now (`require_auth_and_message`) instead of decorator magic. Same dedup, less indirection risk in async handlers.
- `+ #3 _record_blackboard`: implement now. Good dedup and easier future backend extension.
- `- #4 delete parse_backend_request`: do **not** delete now; tests and possible external callers still use it. Keep as compatibility shim, mark deprecated.
- `+ #5 response formatting cleanup`: implement now.
- `- #6 setdefault for lock`: reject. `setdefault(..., asyncio.Lock())` constructs a lock every call; current explicit form is safer/clearer.
- `~ #7 simplify get_reply_message with or`: partial. Add return type annotation now, keep explicit `is not None` logic for safety.
- `+ #8 return type annotation`: implement now (`-> Message | None`).
- `- #9 remove redundant or ""`: defer. Keeping null-tolerant cleanup is defensive hardening, not harmful complexity.

**Premise Check**
- Cutting ~100 LOC is not the real complexity win.
- Real complexity is control-flow branching across auth, routing, queueing, and blackboard side effects.
- Prioritize simplifications that reduce branching and side-effect duplication, not just line count.

**Reliability Guardrails**
- Add regression tests before refactor:
  - Unauthorized command behavior across all handlers.
  - `parse_backend_request` compatibility.
  - Blackboard writes for `/codex` and broadcast turns.
  - Lock identity/stability per chat.
- Roll out in 2 commits:
  1. Pure helpers + no behavior change.
  2. Handler rewiring to helper/decorator equivalent.
- Keep `parse_backend_request` for one release with deprecation note in docstring.

**Radical Option (risky, high payoff)**
- Replace per-command branching with one `TurnContext` pipeline:
  - `ingest -> auth -> route -> execute -> persist -> render`.
- Move backend-specific behavior behind a `BackendRunner` interface (`claude`, `codex`) so routing has zero backend `if/else`.
- Split [`mopsus/agent.py`](/Users/v/Code%202026/heated-debate/mopsus/agent.py) into `config.py`, `routing.py`, `handlers.py`, `backends/`, `blackboard.py`.
- Risk: larger change surface now; payoff: major future reliability and testability gains.

If you want, I can produce a concrete “Phase 1 patch plan” (function-by-function edit list + corresponding test deltas) in diff format next.

Turn 1 - Assistant
**Findings**
1. High: `#4` rationale is weak. In-repo usage of `parse_backend_request` is only tests; runtime uses `parse_backend_request_details` ([agent.py:641](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py:641), [test_mopsus.py:362](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/tests/test_mopsus.py:362)). Keeping dead API “for possible external callers” is speculative debt unless you declare a real deprecation window.
2. Medium: `#2` “helper not decorator” is directionally right, but still too timid. Auth/message preamble is duplicated in 5 handlers ([agent.py:899](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py:899), [agent.py:914](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py:914), [agent.py:943](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py:943), [agent.py:990](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py:990), [agent.py:1110](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py:1110)). Do one gate helper now, not partial dedup.
3. Medium: `#6` debate misses the real issue. `setdefault` alloc overhead is trivial; bigger reliability risk is unbounded `_chat_locks` growth ([agent.py:885](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py:885)). Add lock lifecycle/eviction plan.
4. Low: deferring `#9` keeps type-contract blur in `_clean_blackboard_text` ([agent.py:385](/Users/v/Code%202026/tweets/mopsus/agent.py:385)). Better to enforce `str` at boundaries and simplify now.

**Decision Revision (diff)**
```diff
+ #1 _env_choice: implement now.
~ #2 auth dedup: implement now as plain helper (not decorator), and apply to all command handlers in one pass.
+ #3 _record_blackboard: implement now.
- #4 keep parse_backend_request “for external callers”.
+ #4 either delete now + update tests, or keep with explicit DeprecationWarning + removal date.
+ #5 response formatting cleanup: implement now.
~ #6 keep explicit _get_lock (or setdefault, either is fine), but add lock-eviction follow-up.
~ #7 keep explicit `is not None` logic; do not switch to `or`.
+ #8 add `-> Message | None`.
+ #9 implement now; remove redundant `or ""`.
```

**Radical (risky)**
1. Kill broadcast-by-default; single backend per turn, explicit `/both` for dual-run. Massive reliability gain, less side-effect coupling.
2. Replace handler branching with a `TurnContext` pipeline (`ingest/auth/route/execute/persist/render`) plus backend plugins.

Turn 2 - User
[Creativity: 4/5] Suggest improvements and alternatives. Challenge assumptions. Consider non-obvious solutions.

Your revision is strong. One assumption to challenge: `_chat_locks` is effectively bounded today because auth gates to one configured `chat_id`, so lock-eviction is not urgent unless multi-chat support is planned.

Revised call:

1. Implement now: `#1`, `#2` (plain helper, not decorator), `#3`, `#5`, `#8`, `#9`.
2. `#4`: choose one explicit path now.
   - Preferred: delete `parse_backend_request` and update tests.
   - Conservative: keep shim with `DeprecationWarning` and hard removal date (for example, April 1, 2026).
3. `#6`: keep explicit `_get_lock` for clarity or use `setdefault`; reliability impact is negligible either way.
4. `#7`: keep explicit `is not None` logic; add return type annotation without switching to `or`.

Non-obvious reliability simplification to consider now:

1. Stop broadcast-by-default and require explicit dual-run (`/both` or prefix). This removes the highest side-effect multiplier.
2. Introduce a small `TurnContext` object and one shared `process_turn()` path used by `/codex` and text handling. This shrinks branching more than line-level cleanup.
3. Add one policy test: “one user input -> exactly N blackboard writes where N = selected backends + user row.” That catches most regressions from refactors.

If you want, I can draft a concrete phase plan with exact function signatures and test edits.
